#VU Subject types for v1.37 by SF
#Credits go to: Prussia, Don, Altan, Letole and Modus
# OBS! Full modding not supported. Code support still needed to remove/rename the original subject types.
# Custom ones CAN be created with scriptable diplomatic actions (see "dummy" at the bottom of this file), although this is not currently very functional.

# If used, copy_from should be put at the very top ( things above it will be overwitten )

# Triggers will be evaluated in the scope of the Subject, with the Overlord as its FROM scope.
# Exception: is_potential_overlord is evaluated in the scope of the potential Overlord, with no particular subject in mind.

# count = x is used (means it "counts as" x in some triggers).

# copy_from copies everything except count, is_potential_overlord, and can_be_established

# relative_power_class decides how Subjects are grouped together when considering relative strenghth towards overlord:
# If it is 0 they won't consider relative power and if it is 1 they will only consider their own power (and those supporting their independence) compared to their Overlord's.
# Otherwise they will sum up the power of every Subject of the same relative_power_class as themselves, and all countries who support either themselves or one of their allies in the same relative_power_class.

# diplomacy_view_class decides how subjects are grouped together in diplomacy view and in foreign province view:
# 0 means it won't be listed
# 1 means it will be listed together only with the same subject type
# Other values means it will be listed together with all subjects of the same diplomacy_view_class

# The following status checks are considered in old triggers:

# is_colonial_nation  & is_former_colonial_nation
#        checks the 'has_colonial_parent = yes' attribute

# is_lesser_in_union, junior_union_with, senior_union_with & years_in_union_under
#		checks the 'has_overlords_ruler = yes' attribute
# Forward declaring all subject types so they can refer to each other in triggers etc. (Not sure if it's necessary but I like to have a list at the start of the file as in 00_subject_types) By Altan

viceroyalty_vu = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_court_union
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_leadunions
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_inunion

    # Properties:
    can_release_and_play = yes
    overlord_can_attack = no
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    press_sailors = yes
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.1

    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.10
    cities_required_for_bonuses = 10
    military_focus = 0.75

    relative_power_class = 2

    restoration_cb = cb_restore_personal_union

    # Subject Interactions:
    placate_rulers = no
    divert_trade = yes
    replace_governor = yes
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    support_loyalists = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = vassal_nation
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = large_colonial_nation
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 10
        }
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = in_union
    subject_opinion_modifier = in_union
}

#Basically a non-voluntary tributary, but who gives no tribute.... in other words, pretty much worthless. Papal States' goal will be to convert these to vassals via decision, or possibly an event or two.
papal_subject_vu = {
    #Note from tributary state entry - If similar subject added check if it needs to be added to these scripted triggers: is_subject_except_tributary_trigger, is_free_or_tributary_trigger . Thanks Paradox person!
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_papal_vassal
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_papal_leadclients
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_papal_areclients

    # Properties:
    transfer_trade_power = no
    joins_overlords_wars = no
    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    has_power_projection = yes
    uses_military_focus = yes
    overlord_protects_external = yes
    can_use_claims = no
    share_rebel_popup = no
    can_transfer_in_peace = no
    can_set_mil_focus = yes

    #max_government_rank = 6
    trust_on_start = 10

    relative_power_class = 1

    can_fight = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = papal_subject_vu
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_rival = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = papal_subject_vu
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_ally = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = papal_subject_vu
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_marry = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = papal_subject_vu
        other_overlord = all
    }

    # Subject Interactions
    #Disabling
    embargo_rivals = no
    placate_rulers = no
    knowledge_sharing = no

    #Enabling
    support_loyalists = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes

    # Modifiers

    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = { modifier = subject_nation }
    modifier_overlord = clear

    overlord_opinion_modifier = vu_is_papal_subject
    subject_opinion_modifier = vu_is_papal_subject
}

hanseatic_league_member_vu = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_vassal
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_leadvassal
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_amvassal

    # Properties:
    takes_diplo_slot = no #Modified
    can_be_annexed = yes
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes

    max_government_rank = 6

    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.20
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -5.0
    pays_overlord = 1.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.1

    relative_power_class = 2

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_vassal

    # Subject Interactions:
    scutage = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    seize_territory = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = vassal_nation
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = vassal_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
}

silesian_duke = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_silesian_duke
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_leadsilesian_duke
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_amsilesian_duke

    # Properties:
    can_fight_independence_war = yes
    transfer_trade_power = yes
    joins_colonial_wars = no
    is_voluntary = no
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    can_be_annexed = yes
    can_transfer_in_peace = yes
    can_release_in_peace = yes
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    overlord_protects_external = yes
    counts_for_borders = yes
    can_use_claims = yes
    can_set_mil_focus = yes
    can_send_missionary_to_subject = yes
    overlord_can_fabricate_for = yes
    does_overlord_size_count_for_warscore_cost = no
    can_concentrate_development = no

    max_government_rank = 6
    cities_required_for_bonuses = 0
    trust_on_start = 35

    base_liberty_desire = -20.0
    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 10.0
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -5.0
    liberty_desire_revolution = 35.0
    pays_overlord = 1.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.15

    relative_power_class = 2

    can_fight = { # Silesian dukes can fight between each other
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = march
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = march
    }

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_vassal

    # Subject Interactions:
    scutage = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    seize_territory = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    placate_rulers = yes
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    takeondebt = yes
    knowledge_sharing = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = silesian_duke_modifier
    }

    modifier_subject = { # Actually penalities vassal recieves for being too large since silesian duchies were rather small and fractured
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 5
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 7
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 10
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 14
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }

    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = vassal_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
}

selucid_satrapy = {
    copy_from = vassal
    count = vassal

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gives_daimyo_bonuses = yes
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    can_use_claims = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no

    trust_on_start = 0

    base_liberty_desire = 10.0
    military_focus = 1.2

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    # Subject Interactions
    #(disable)
    scutage = no
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = no
    enforce_religion = no
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    force_seppuku = no
    contribute_to_capital = no
    conscript_general = no
    force_isolation = no
    return_land = no
    #(special)
    sword_hunt = no
    sankin_kotai = no
    expel_ronin = no

    # Modifiers

    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_nation
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = daimyo_subject
    }
}

    # Graphics:

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_amcanton

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = { has_country_flag = can_make_canton }

    # Properties:
    can_fight_independence_war = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    overlord_can_be_subject = yes
    can_be_annexed = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    can_release_in_peace = yes
    counts_for_borders = yes
    can_use_claims = yes
    share_rebel_popup = yes
    can_set_mil_focus = yes
    overlord_can_fabricate_for = yes
    base_liberty_desire = 0.0
    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 0.0
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.2
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -10.0
    pays_overlord = 1.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.25
    manpower_to_overlord = 0.1
    relative_power_class = 1
    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_vassal
    #
    # Subject Interactions:
    scutage = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    #sacrifice_ruler = yes #???? Aztects of Europe
    #sacrifice_heir = yes
    divert_trade = yes
    #seize_territory = yes
    embargo_rivals = yes
    #send_officers = yes
    placate_rulers = yes
    takeondebt = yes
    knowledge_sharing = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = vassal_nation
    }
    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = vassal_subject
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = swi_canton_republican_ties_modifier
    }
    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
}

#VU 1.37 ToR additions by SF
#AUTONOMOUS CANTON
autonomous_canton = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_autonomous_canton
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_leadautonomous_canton
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_amautonomous_canton

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = { has_country_flag = can_make_autonomous_canton } 			# This part is not copied in copy_from. Actual default is equivalent to always = yes

    # Properties:
    can_fight_independence_war = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    overlord_can_be_subject = yes
    can_be_annexed = no
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    can_release_in_peace = yes
    counts_for_borders = yes
    can_use_claims = yes
    share_rebel_popup = yes
    can_set_mil_focus = yes
    overlord_can_fabricate_for = yes
    base_liberty_desire = 0.0
    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 0.0
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.2
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -10.0
    pays_overlord = 1.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.25
    manpower_to_overlord = 0.1
    relative_power_class = 1
    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_vassal
    #
    # Subject Interactions:
    scutage = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    divert_trade = no

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_marquisate #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = marquisate_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = marquisate_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_marquisate
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_marquisate

    takes_diplo_slot = no

    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no

    trust_on_start = 0

    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = austrian_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = austrian_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = austrian_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = austrian_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    # Subject Interactions:

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_marquisate #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

        modifier = marquisate_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {

                religion = PREV
            }

    grant_core_claim = yes

    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no

    #(enable)

    return_land = yes

    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = no
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    # Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_principality #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = principality_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = principality_subject

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_hungarian_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = hungarian_barony
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = hungarian_barony
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = hungarian_barony
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = hungarian_barony
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = baronial_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = baronial_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_barony
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_barony
}

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_italian_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_core_eyalet

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 0.5
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = italian_county
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = italian_county
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = italian_county
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = italian_county
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = earldom_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = earldom_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_county
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_county
}

    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_norwegian_aristocracy
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_norwegian_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = norwegian_barony
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = norwegian_barony
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = norwegian_barony
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = norwegian_barony
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = baronial_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = baronial_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_barony
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_barony
}

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_polish_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_core_eyalet

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 0.5
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = polish_county
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = polish_county
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = polish_county
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = polish_county
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = earldom_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = earldom_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_county
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_county
}

    return_land = yes

    # Modifiers

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_marquisate #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = marquisate_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = marquisate_subject
    }

    subject_opinion_modifier = is_marquisate

    sprite = GFX_icon_portuguese_duchy #Was GFX_icon_core_eyalet
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_portuguese_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_core_eyalet
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_portuguese_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_core_eyalet

    # Properties:
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.1
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 20.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 0.25
    can_be_integrated = yes #Changed from can_be_annexed = yes - SF & Prussia
    can_be_annexed = no
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes


    # Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = yes
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = no
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    # Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_duchy #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = duchy_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = duchy_historic_naval_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_duchy
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_duchy
}

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_prussian_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = prussian_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = prussian_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = prussian_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = prussian_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto

    }

swedish_lordship = {
    copy_from = default

    sprite = GFX_icon_swedish_lordship
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_swedish_aristocracy
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_swedish_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = swedish_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = swedish_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = swedish_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = swedish_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = lordship_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = lordship_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
}

anglois_crown_PU = {
    copy_from = personal_union

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_court_anglois_union
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_anglois_diplomacy_leadunions
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_anglois_diplomacy_inunion

    # Properties:
    has_overlords_ruler = yes
    can_be_integrated = yes
    overlord_can_attack = no
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes
    can_union_break = no
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    transfer_subjects_when_made = yes
    can_concentrate_development = no
    extend_trading_range = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 1.0
    military_focus = 0.66

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    restoration_cb = cb_restore_personal_union

    # Subject Interactions:
    placate_rulers = no
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    support_loyalists = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = anglois_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = anglois_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = anglois_crown_pu_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = in_union
    subject_opinion_modifier = in_union
}

    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes

        modifier = prussian_crown_pu_bonus

#CANADIAN PROVINCES
canadian_province_subject_vu = {
    copy_from = default
    count = vassal

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_canadian_provinces_subject #Was GFX_icon_dutch_province_subject
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_lead_canadian_provinces_subject #Was GFX_diplomacy_leaddutch_province_subject
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_am_canadian_provinces_subject #Was GFX_diplomacy_amdutch_province_subject

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = {
        is_subject = yes
        OR = {
            primary_culture = quebecois
            primary_culture = canadian
        }
        capital_scope = {
            region = canada_region
        }
        NOT = {
            any_country = {
                NOT = { tag = PREV }
                has_subject_of_type = canadian_province_subject_vu #Was dutch_province_subject
            }
        }
        NOT = {
            calc_true_if = {
                all_subject_country = {
                    is_subject_of_type = canadian_province_subject_vu #Was dutch_province_subject
                }
                amount = 5
            }
        }
    }

    # Properties:
    transfer_trade_if_merchant_republic = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    overlord_can_attack = no
    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    overlord_protects_external = yes
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    can_transfer_in_peace = no
    does_overlord_size_count_for_warscore_cost = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    can_have_great_projects_moved_by_overlord = no
    can_be_annexed = no

    base_liberty_desire = -10.0
    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 0.25
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.33
    pays_overlord = 1.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0

    relative_power_class = 1
    diplomacy_view_class = 1

    should_quit_wars_on_activation = no

    can_fight = {
        independent_nations = yes
        other_overlord = all
        same_overlord = canadian_province_subject_vu #Was dutch_province_subject
    }
    can_rival = {
        independent_nations = yes
        other_overlord = all
        same_overlord = canadian_province_subject_vu
    }
    can_ally = {
        independent_nations = yes
        other_overlord = all
        same_overlord = canadian_province_subject_vu
    }
    can_marry = {
        independent_nations = yes
        other_overlord = all
        same_overlord = canadian_province_subject_vu
    }

    # Subject Interactions:
    # (continuous)
    scutage = yes
    divert_trade = yes
    # (immediate)
    placate_rulers = no
    enforce_religion = no
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    grant_core_claim = no
    takeondebt = yes
    bestow_gifts = yes
    block_settlement_growth = no
    allow_settlement_growth = no

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = canadian_province_subject_modifier #Was dutch_province_subject_modifier
    }

    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = canadian_province_subject_overlord_modifier #Was dutch_province_subject_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            has_global_flag = canadian_province_subject_no_leader_election #Was dutch_province_subject_no_leader_election
            marriage_with = FROM
        }
        modifier = royal_marriage_no_slot_cost_modifier
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_canadian_province_subject #Was is_dutch_province_subject
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_canadian_province_subject #Was is_dutch_province_subject
}

#TURKISH TRIBUTARY BEYLIK
turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal = {
    #Functions like a Daimyo/Vassal/Tributary in that it is allowed to attack other vassals of the Turks. It also has to give taxes in the form of Jizya and it must give manpower to its overlord in times of war.
    copy_from = default
    can_have_great_projects_moved_by_overlord = no

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = {
        OR = {
            has_reform = ottoman_government
            technology_group = ottoman
            culture_group = turkish_g
        }
    }

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_subject_turkish_tributary_state
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_turkish_leadtributary
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_turkish_amtributary

    # Properties:
    can_fight_independence_war = yes
    can_be_annexed = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    joins_colonial_wars = no
    overlord_can_attack = no
    takes_diplo_slot = yes
    base_liberty_desire = -5
    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = no
    can_send_tribute = yes
    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes
    uses_military_focus = no
    overlord_protects_external = yes
    counts_for_borders = no
    can_use_claims = no
    share_rebel_popup = yes
    can_transfer_in_peace = yes
    can_set_mil_focus = no
    can_send_missionary_to_subject = no
    overlord_can_fabricate_for = no
    does_overlord_size_count_for_warscore_cost = no
    can_concentrate_development = no

    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.175
    trust_on_start = 0

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal

    can_fight = {
        independent_nations = no
        same_overlord = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_rival = {
        independent_nations = no
        same_overlord = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_ally = {
        independent_nations = no
        same_overlord = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_marry = {
        independent_nations = no
        same_overlord = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal
        other_overlord = all
    }

    # Subject Interactions:
    # (immediate)
    enforce_religion = no
    grant_core_claim = no
    bestow_gifts = yes
    send_additional_troops = no
    demand_artifacts = no
    demand_additional_tribute = yes
    request_extra_levies = yes
    block_settlement_growth = yes
    allow_settlement_growth = no
    placate_rulers = yes
    knowledge_sharing = no
    siphon_income = yes
    # (continuous)
    embargo_rivals = yes

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal_subject_modifier #Was tributary_state_behind_overlord_tech_adm
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = turkish_tributary_beylik_vassal_overlord_modifier #Was hordes_tributary_state_tribute
    }
}

                has_government_attribute = pirate_vassal_bonus
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = GER_extra_prov_trade_power
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_GER_customs_union
            }
        }
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_feudal_republic #Was is_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_feudal_republic #Was is_vassal

#MERCHANTLIST REPUBLIC
merchantlist_republic = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_merchantlist_republic
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_merchantlist_republic_leadvassal
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_merchantlist_republic_amvassal

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = {
        is_subject = no
        OR = {
            AND = {
                culture_group = latin
                has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
            }
            # Custom Rule
            has_government_attribute = can_create_merchantlist_republic_rule
        }
    }

    # Properties:
    transfer_trade_power = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    extend_trading_range = yes
    can_be_annexed = no

    max_government_rank = 6
    cities_required_for_bonuses = 0
    trust_on_start = 35

    base_liberty_desire = -10
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.15
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -5.0
    liberty_desire_revolution = 0
    pays_overlord = 0.25
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.05

    relative_power_class = 6
    diplomacy_view_class = 1

    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
    }
    can_rival = {
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = merchantlist_republic
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = feudal_republic
        same_overlord = merchantlist_republic
        same_overlord = venetian_republic
        same_overlord = genoese_commercial_republic
    }

    # Subject Interactions:
    # (continuous)
    scutage = yes
    # (immediate)
    seize_territory = yes
    contribute_to_capital = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_nation
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_IS_MERCHANT_REPUBLIC_TT
                has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_merchant_republic_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            capital_scope = {
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HOME_NODE_HAS_MERCHANT_FROM_OVERLORD_TT
                    has_merchant = FROM
                }
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_overlord_trading_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_seized_merchant_fleets_modifier
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HAS_SEIZE_MERCHANT_FLEETS_TT
                has_country_flag = merchantlist_republic_seize_merchant_fleets
            }
        }
    }

    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            capital_scope = {
                OR = {
                    trade_share = {
                        country = ROOT
                        share = 50
                    }
                    custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                        tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HOME_NODE_OVERLORD_HAS_75_TRADE_POWER_TT
                        trade_share = {
                            country = FROM
                            share = 75
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_merchant_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_seized_merchant_fleets_overlord_modifier
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HAS_SEIZE_MERCHANT_FLEETS_TT
                has_country_flag = merchantlist_republic_seize_merchant_fleets
            }
            NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
        }
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_merchantlist_republic
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_merchantlist_republic
}

    sprite = GFX_icon_islamic_sheikdom
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_islamic_subjects
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_islamic_subjects

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = islamic_sheikdom
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = islamic_sheikdom
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = islamic_sheikdom
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = islamic_sheikdom
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = sheikdom_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = sheikdom_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_sheikdom
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_sheikdom
}

#SELF-GOVERNING DOMINION
self_governing_dominion_vu = {

    copy_from = self_governing_colony

    sprite = GFX_dominion_icon

    change_colonial_type = no
    upgrade_subject_type = yes
    is_colony_subtype = no
    count = colony

    # Properties:
    base_liberty_desire = -10.0
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.05
    pays_overlord = 1.5
    max_government_rank = 8
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.0 			#Changed from 0.05 to reflect a dominion's much greater autonomy
    manpower_to_overlord = 0.0 				#Changed from 0.05
    naval_forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.1		#Changed from 0.05
    sailors_to_overlord = 0.0 				#Changed from 0.05

    # Subject Interactions:
    uses_tariffs = no
    increase_tariffs = no
    decrease_tariffs = no
    divert_trade = yes
    customize_subject = no
    replace_governor = no
    block_settlement_growth = no
    allow_settlement_growth = no
    press_sailors = no
    start_colonial_war = no
    enforce_culture = yes #Although it doesn't make much sense, it functions as a workaround to colonial nations switching to native cultures
    transfer_trade_power = no

    is_potential_overlord = {
        is_subject = no
        OR = {
            is_year = 1600
            current_age = age_of_absolutism
        }
    }

    can_fight = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = tributary_state
        other_overlord = all
    }

    can_rival = {
        independent_nations = yes
        same_overlord = tributary_state
        other_overlord = all
    }
    can_ally = {
        neighboring_primitives = yes
    }

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = self_governing_dominion_vu_overlord
    }

    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = self_governing_dominion_vu_subject
    }
}
